posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:The hotel is located a short walk (~10 minutes with luggage) from the Kunming Railway Station and was easy to find. The staff are very sweet and friendly, especially the breakfast service staff. The breakfast buffet selection was extensive and delicious!

Although we stayed on a non-smoking floor, the corridors do smell of smoke unfortunately. However once you get inside the room it is smoke-free. The hotel is a bit dated and the pool was under renovation during our stay. The shower includes shower gel and shampoo, but the conditioner is tucked away in a drawer which was a bit confusing to us as we almost didn't find it. The toilet was leaking so there was a constant puddle in the bathroom (thankfully it was clean water). They charged for the water bottles in the room, which was disappointing as we did not experience this in any other hotel in Yunnan during our stay.

msg:Kunming Jiahua Plaza Hotel is an old five-star hotel. But the concept of management is still not out of date.
Reflected in: 1) Very user-friendly. I arrived at 12 noon and was immediately assigned to the 29th floor according to my request to live in a high-rise. Ctrip points can be used to redeem benefits when leaving the hotel, and check-out is allowed before 3 p.m.; breakfast starts at 6:30, which provides convenience for many guests who are catching the train. Since I had not made a reservation in advance, but I wanted to taste the authentic Yunnan Crossing the Bridge Rice Noodles, the front desk helped me make a reservation. The basic version was only 58 yuan per serving, which was full of enjoyment and aftertaste. 2) The service is attentive. The canopy swimming pool on the seventh floor has a ceiling. The afterglow of the sunset is very interesting for taking pictures. The water quality and temperature are impeccable. The two waiters, Xiao Luo and Xiao Li, were enthusiastic, thoughtful, and serious about their work. They enthusiastically provided drinking water and towels, and the experience was very warm.
3) Safety first. The swimming pool regulations are strict, and the water quality testing and rescue procedures are clear. I was criticized by the waiter for wearing the slippers in the room during breakfast and pointed out the potential risks, which I accepted humbly.
The room is clean, the bedding is comfortable, and free and paid mineral water are provided for your choice, both in the shower and in the bathtub.
The transportation is even more convenient. It only takes 8 minutes to walk to Kunming Station. This time I took the 8:18 am train to Shilin. There is also a direct bus to Dianchi Lake. A taxi to Kunming Old Street costs about 9 yuan. You can also walk to the Golden Horse and Jade Rooster, which is very convenient.
The lobby, Chinese restaurant (Tianbao Pavilion) and Western restaurant of Kunming Jiahua Plaza Hotel are grand, clean and memorable.
Yunnan's colorful beauty and simple folk customs can be fully enjoyed in "Jiahua"!

msg:I am a photography enthusiast, and I always want to take some cityscape photos when I live in a hotel. Jiahua Plaza Hotel is very good at meeting your needs. Different from other high-rise hotels, every room in Jiahua has a half-meter-wide down-opening window that can be opened and hands can be stretched out, which is very important for those who pursue high-definition photos. The hotel's doorman, lobby manager, front desk clerk, and restaurant clerk are very polite, worthy of a five-star hotel. We lived in an executive city-view twin room on the 32nd floor facing north. The unique feature of this floor is that there is a 10 cm wide window sill outside the window, which can be used to put a small tripod, which is very beneficial for taking high-quality time-lapse photography. The hotel's breakfast is rich, duck breast and yogurt are impressive. For the "all you can eat" event at 108 yuan per person for lunch, the two of us ordered five dishes, all of which tasted good, and basically finished them all. For the second dinner, I ordered two sets, the spicy tofu set and the black pepper beef tenderloin set, which must be praised. The only disadvantage of the hotel is that it is not soundproof. It is recommended to install a sealing ***** on the door. On the second night of our stay at Jiahua, in order to be quieter and to take pictures from more angles, we asked to change rooms. The attitude of the hotel is very good. Although there is no room of the same type, in order to meet our requirements, we will give We were upgraded to an executive suite facing south on the 24th floor. The rain shower in the hotel has a large amount of water and the water temperature is comfortable. The sanitary ware is Kohler's. It's a pity that there is no cushion when the toilet lid falls, and the sound is loud. The condition of the gym and swimming pool is very good, worthy of being a time-honored five-star hotel.

msg:The hotel has been upgraded and turned into family suites which are huge.
But the layout is not good, it is at the end of the corridor, and the room is not bright. Various corners.

The bathroom is large, the shower is sufficient, and the hot water is full. There is also a large bathtub, double toilets, and a large washstand. I am satisfied~ very good.

The location of the hotel is good. It takes 2 minutes to walk to the subway entrance. There are many people who come here for meetings. 540 a night.
Let me talk about some bugs:
1. The air conditioner and the sound are relatively loud, so you can only turn it off when you sleep at night.
2. The wifi here is useless.
3. The sound insulation effect is not good, and the next door takes a shower at night, rumbling.
4. There is only one food delivery robot in such a big hotel?
5. The pillows are too bad. There are only two pillows on such a big bed, usually four, and two cushions. These two pillows are basically suffocated after lying down for a while.
6. The bathroom can be locked from the inside. If you accidentally touch it inside, and then close the door, you will not be able to open it from the outside!
7. There is no suitable socket for the hair dryer in the bathroom, and there is no socket for the kettle. Finally, find the socket under the table and boil water on the ground!
